   <script type="text/javascript">
    window.SETUPS = window.SETUPS || (
 		function () {
 			let __ = {},
 				exports = {__: __};
 			__.stored = {};
 
 			exports.set = function (key, value) {
 				__.stored[key] = value;
 			};
 
 			exports.unset = function (key) {
 				if (key in __.stored) {
 					delete __.stored[key];
 					return true;
 				}
 				else {
 					return false;
 				}
 			};
 
 			exports.get = function (key) {
 				return __.stored[key] || null;
 			};
 
 			return exports;
 		}());
   </script>
   <script type="text/javascript">
    window.audi = window.audi || {};
 	window.audi.api = window.audi.api || {};
 	window.audi.api.lastConfiguration = window.audi.api.lastConfiguration || function () {
 		let _storage = window.localStorage;
 
 		if (!!_storage && _storage.lastConfiguration) {
 			try {
 				return JSON.parse(_storage.lastConfiguration);
 			}
 			catch (err) {
 				console.warn(err);
 				return false;
 			}
 		}
 		else {
 			return false;
 		}
 	};
   </script>
